                    <span style="font-family:open sans,sans-serif;">
                     <span style="color:#002E5D;">

                   </span>

                  <p class="font_8" style="font-size:14px;">

                     <span style="color:#002E5D;">
                      Brentham Cricket Club offers four competitive Saturday XI's playing league cricket in Middlesex,and two Sunday teams playing Cup, friendly and SundayLeague cricket.
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </span>
                  </p>
